   00 | ------ IMark(0x400008, 4, 1) ------
   01 | t0 = GET:I32(itstate)
   02 | t1 = Shr32(t0,0x08)
   03 | t740 = And32(t0,0x000000f0)
   04 | t739 = Xor32(t740,0x000000e0)
   05 | t741 = GET:I32(cc_op)
   06 | t738 = Or32(t741,t739)
   07 | t742 = GET:I32(cc_dep1)
   08 | t743 = GET:I32(cc_dep2)
   09 | t744 = GET:I32(cc_ndep)
   10 | t745 = armg_calculate_condition(t738,t742,t743,t744):Ity_I32
   11 | t747 = CmpNE32(t740,0x00000000)
   12 | t746 = ITE(t747,t745,0x00000001)
   13 | t753 = GET:I32(r8)
   14 | t752 = And32(t753,0x0000ffff)
